class=\"site-content\">\n\n\t\t<div class=\"top-section\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\n\t\t<div class=\"container main-content-area\">\n            \t\t\t<div class=\"row pull-left\">\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"main-content-inner col-sm-12 col-md-8\">\n\n\t<div id=\"primary\" class=\"content-area\">\n\t\t<main id=\"main\" class=\"site-main\" role=\"main\">\n\n\t\t\n<article id=\"post-62328\" class=\"post-62328 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-other-writers\">\n\t\t<div class=\"post-inner-content\">\n\t\t<header class=\"entry-header page-header\">\n\n\t\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title \">A Cry from California \u2014 &#8216;God help us all!&#8217;</h1>\n\n\t\t\t<div class=\"entry-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t<span class=\"byline\"> <i class=\"fa fa-user fa-2x\"></i> <span class=\"author vcard\"><a class=\"url fn n\" href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/author/admin/\">Admin</a></span></span><span class=\"posted-on\"><i class=\"fa fa-calendar\"></i> <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/\" rel=\"bookmark\"><time class=\"entry-date published\" datetime=\"2017-03-09T06:00:54+00:00\">March 9, 2017</time><time class=\"updated\" datetime=\"2017-03-09T09:43:42+00:00\">March 9, 2017</time></a></span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"cat-links\"><i class=\"fa fa-folder-open-o\"></i>\n\t\t\t\t\t <a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/category/other-writers/\" rel=\"category tag\">Other Writers</a>\t\t\t\t</span>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div><!-- .entry-meta -->\n\t\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t\t<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong>By <span style=\"color: #800000;\"><em>KAPOORE<br/>\n</em></span></strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><img class=\"aligncenter wp-image-62330\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/642x453xPicture1-1.png.pagespeed.ic.WLzpwGf33r.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"642\" height=\"453\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Picture1-1.png 939w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Picture1-1-150x106.png 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Picture1-1-300x212.png 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Picture1-1-768x542.png 768w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/Picture1-1-600x424.png 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 642px) 100vw, 642px\"/></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>(1) FAR LEFT: Chief Heather Fong, first San Francisco Police Department<em> lesbian</em> chief of police.</strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>(2) CENTER:\u00a0 Theresa Sparks, transgender female who started out life as a man, is president of San Francisco Police Commission and CEO of a multi-million dollar sex toy retailer.</strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>(3) FAR RIGHT: Sgt. Stephan Thorne, former female, the first transgender male San Francisco Police Department officer \u2014 once a pretty gal, now a guy with a mustache.\u00a0</strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\"><strong>Is it any wonder that people in California are a bit confused?\u00a0</strong><span id=\"more-62328\"></span></p>\n<hr/>\n<p><strong>I was getting my granddaughter to sleep</strong> and we were lying in bed together reading stories. She suddenly got this funny look on her face and said, <em>\u201cLet\u2019s play a tickle game.\u201d</em> She began naming my body parts. I said that I didn\u2019t like tickle games and I put the whole thing to a stop by reading her another story. But the incident disturbed me. She spends half the time with her father, although she is barely three years old. He without a doubt is a heavy watcher of porn and is well acquainted with the wild side of Los Angeles. He is obviously sexually turned on by her. Smitten with his own daughter.</p>\n<p>Should an adult male who watches porn be playing tickling game with his three year old daughter? That&#8217;s a rhetorical question. I already know the answer. I&#8217;m talking about my granddaughter here&#8230; and I can tell you, I don&#8217;t like this situation one little bit.</p>\n<p>But what can I do about it?</p>\n<p>Even if I could do something about this guy, my granddaughter is probably better off where she is than if she got taken into protective custody. She&#8217;s a blonde, you see, \u00a0and I guess that carries an extra price.<em> YUCK!!</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">We\u2019ll know whether Trump is going to succeed or fail in cleaning the swamp when it comes to prosecution of certain high profile people in the Clinton camp like John Podesta, who is rumored to be an evil pedophile. I pray that the Washington pedophile ring aligned with the Clintons faces justice soon\u2026 very soon. This is urgent!!</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>My Jewish mother in law</strong> lived in New York and would come to visit once a year with a suitcase of frozen food because she wouldn\u2019t eat in my house since I was too <em>treif</em>, that is non-kosher. This was although my mother-in-law was not religious and actually disliked Jews. \u00a0Since Jews were the only people she knew, she basically disliked <em>everyone.</em> So\u2026 one year she is coming over to my place for Passover and I go to a deli and get very fancy Passover food to have a Seder. She arrives from her hotel with her normal look of disgust on her face, but once we sat down for the Seder meal she went into flip out mode.</p>\n<p>&#8220;What is this,&#8221; she screams, &#8220;have you people turned into Lubovitchers?&#8221;</p>\n<p>That ended that. Basically, this is a pathological level of criticism where the criticizer never looks in the mirror and yet never stops from the barrage of negative commentary. We see this with the ten commandments of political correctness, the first being that <strong>\u201cThou shalt never criticize Jews.\u201d</strong></p>\n<p>These Jews&#8230; you&#8217;re not allowed to criticize them&#8230; but they get to criticize you until your civilization is dead.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>I lived through the Sixties</strong> and it was not too bad a time. It&#8217;s way worse now. In the sixties, we didn\u2019t have a generation of profoundly sick children, whereas now we have one in 60 children with autism. It&#8217;s as high as one in 21 boys. In a few years&#8217; time it&#8217;s predicted to soar to 50 percent. What are we going to do as a society when every second child is autistic?</p>\n<p>Consider some of these <em>art shows</em>. These are now are called &#8220;spirit cooking events&#8221;. Cakes are made in the form of a <em>corpse</em>. Guests sit around a table with actors playing around with <em>decapitated heads</em>. And everyone watches as half naked men take out these long knives and cut limbs and genitals out of the cake. Then everyone eats, and pretends they&#8217;re having a great time! Hey, I can\u2019t imagine anything like this going on in the Swinging Sixties, can you?\u00a0<em>No way!</em></p>\n<p>Listen to this. It will make you laugh. But it&#8217;s not funny.</p>\n<p>An interviewer in California went round asking random people on the beach what they think of the Trump boys <em>hunting dinosaurs in Africa!</em>\u00a0He shows them a fake picture of the Trump brothers next to a dead dinosaur. People are shocked, genuinely shocked, because dinosaurs are \u201can endangered species.\u201d Hunting dinosaurs to death just isn&#8217;t right!</p>\n<p>The same bogus interviewer tells people on the beach that Bernie Sanders is thinking of having Bernie Madoff (the Ponzi scheme fraudster who stole millions of bucks from his clients) as his Vice President. The ticket would be Bernie and Bernie. &#8220;So what do you folks think of this?&#8221; he asks. Well, it seems these folks think it&#8217;s a darn good idea! It has a nice ring to it.</p>\n<p>In other words, the level of stupidity has reached epic proportions in California. It&#8217;s beyond belief. I&#8217;m wondering if this staggering stupidity has spread like a plague to the rest of America? I wouldn&#8217;t be surprised if it had.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-62431\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/x9eb8b-1.jpg.pagespeed.ic.CY2bytHTJ8.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"627\" height=\"557\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/9eb8b-1.jpg 627w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/9eb8b-1-150x133.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/9eb8b-1-300x267.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/9eb8b-1-600x533.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 627px) 100vw, 627px\"/></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>Donald Trump is</strong> our accidental president. No one thought he would win.<em> He</em> didn\u2019t think he would win, but now for the first time we have the slimmest chance to take back our country.</p>\n<p>Maybe I exaggerate the threat of the neocons and the Israelis because they have been the menace for the entire stretch of my adult life, with all their concocted wars. So I hope that Donald can separate himself from his Jewish son-in-law&#8217;s influence. I\u2019m always hoping and praying there are rational minds at work out there. Let\u2019s pray that rationality takes the day! That sanity returns&#8230;</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">I could write a book on how the Left has let me down.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">I cannot imagine a worse tragedy for our country than to have Hillary Clinton as President, with John Podesta as chief of staff. They talk about Donald Trump being deranged, which I don\u2019t think he is. What about Hillary Clinton? Didn\u2019t she just announce she was going to run for the Presidency again in 2020? Hillary Clinton was apparently too drunk and off her rocker to give her adoring supporters a speech on election night. Hmmm, when someone runs for office, isn\u2019t there always the possibility of losing? Why would a politician be so friggin lame that she can\u2019t DEAL with losing an election?</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: left;\">So\u2026 I always thought they are in the hotel room or wherever and they just turn off the TV and go out and meet their supporters with some comforting words. Hillary couldn\u2019t do that. And people think Donald is the worse of the worst. No, Hillary was the worst of the worst. Thank God we have Trump!</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>Everyone I know</strong> is on the side that wants to take Trump down. I don\u2019t know how they are going to manage it but I wish Trump weren\u2019t so naive, and that he would wake up and just start prosecuting the Hillary nexus, beginning with whatever was on those emails that came out of the Weiner sexting bust.</p>\n<p>But Trump is Trump. He&#8217;s a straight guy, military school graduate, a Fifties dude who goes for locker room talk and the prettiest girl he can find\u2026 He is proud that he led the Israel parade. He hasn\u2019t looked into the dark side of the Democratic party, or the dark side of the Jewish elite. In some ways he is far too naive to be president.</p>\n<p>Yet who else could take on something this vast, this sinister, this lethal than someone who really doesn&#8217;t know what the heck he is doing? So he puts on his red baseball cap, like a knight donning his armor, and off he goes and places himself in front of the disenfranchised and completely destroyed American people. And what does he say? He basically says, &#8220;I am going to lead you out of this dark place!&#8221;</p>\n<p>Oh my\u2026and here we are in the middle of it. <em>God help us!</em></p>\n<p>Are we doomed? I hope not. Of course, no one in Congress or anywhere in the Justice Department \u2013 entirely on board with all this \u2013 has bothered to protect us. I think I heard this from a guy out here in California but I can\u2019t remember his name offhand. Trump has to solicit this type of person for some real help. Trump is so straight that he can\u2019t think the worst of anyone, but he has got to start doing it. And he has to do it in a less open way, from behind the scenes. He&#8217;s got to quit all this tweeting in the wee hours of the morning.</p>\n<p>We need Trump to help us free our bureaucracy from the grip of the corporate fascists and pedophiles. He has to think of what happens to all of us who have been pushed under the bus. Personally, I am not sure what I will do, as I find myself already living here in this corporate fascist hellhole state of California. I know what it\u2019s like to be powerless against multiple mandates. To be forced into buying products in order to make money for Big Pharma. To have politicians that laugh at children who have been poisoned by vaccines and kick out mothers from the halls of government.</p>\n<p>A new word has to be invented for what has happened in California during the last ten years. A gulag? It\u2019s far worse than any gulag here. It&#8217;s beyond anything anyone can imagine. Drunk as skunk politicians passing maniacal laws that stick to the books like glue&#8230;</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\u2014 \u00a0\u00a7 \u00a0\u2014</p>\n<p><strong>I can\u2019t stop</strong>, sorry\u2026 I&#8217;m so upset.</p>\n<p><img class=\"aligncenter size-full wp-image-62435\" src=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/xdreto.jpg.pagespeed.ic.UATXQF_YDE.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"640\" height=\"361\" srcset=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/dreto.jpg 640w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/dreto-150x85.jpg 150w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/dreto-300x169.jpg 300w, https://www.darkmoon.me/uploads/dreto-600x338.jpg 600w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 640px) 100vw, 640px\"/></p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #0000ff;\"><strong>IMAGINE A SOCIETY OF ROBOTS</strong></span></h3>\n<p><strong>People who are so mind controlled they are looking at their phones that tell them the sun is shining.\u00a0And they actually believe the sun is shining, though in fact it\u2019s raining! That\u2019s what we have here in California: a completely brainwashed society of robots. \u00a0</strong></p>\n<p>If their cell phone tells them the weather is fine, that&#8217;s what they come to believe, even when the weather is lousy.</p>\n<p><em>Imagine!</em> \u2014 \u00a0these same people are actually controlled through their cell phones.</p>\n<p>Their every move is potentially charted and plotted through their phones. Imagine that someone is spying on them from a distant computer, and this spook decides that they aren\u2019t sufficiently compliant and politically correct. So what happens? Well, their cars can be blown up, <em>kar-boom!</em> from some remote computer screen!</p>\n<p><em>Whoops!</em> Kapoore is too non-compliant, and she ain&#8217;t behaving like a model citizen, so what happens to Kapoore? \u00a0She\u2019s a good driver, but her car is wired to a satellite &#8230; and so she&#8217;s blown up! <em>Pffooof! </em>Exit<em>\u00a0</em>Kapoore, like puff of smoke. Too bad. Life was good while it lasted.</p>\n<p>Finally, imagine the most heartless, materialistic, spirit cooking pedophile sadists in charge of the network. They drain the lifeblood of children like vampires to extend their own pathetic lives.</p>\n<h3>S &#8211; I &#8211; C &#8211; K!!!</h3>\n<p><em>Please God, don\u2019t let Trump fail!</em></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\">\n<!-- Simple Share Buttons Adder (6.3.4) simplesharebuttons.com --><div class=\"ssba ssba-wrap\"><div style=\"text-align:center\">Like this? Now that we have destroyed these goyim, the danger to us has passed. Let us now attend to our own people and elevate them to the status these people once achieved. </p>\n<p>Our agents learned many secrets from these people, secrets of their science and military technology. Let us now use that knowledge to advance our own military power and build our own cities and with this power we shall project our demands upon the less intelligent people that remain.</p></blockquote>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/?replytocom=948953#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( \"div-comment-948953\", \"948953\", \"respond\", \"62328\" )' aria-label='Reply to Arch Stanton'>Reply</a></div>\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n<ol class=\"children\">\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-949006\" class=\"comment even depth-3\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-949006\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/02c42e0c97dc00f6e3514f7c7fce5828?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/02c42e0c97dc00f6e3514f7c7fce5828?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">John Kirby</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/#comment-949006\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-10T16:12:28+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 10, 2017 at 4:12 pm\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Hi Arch,<br/>\n             I enjoy your articles but I am an optimist. They have all been on bloated salaries at our expense.</p>\n<p>Trust the people.</p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n</li><!-- #comment-## -->\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-949140\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-3\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-949140\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d70bea2070d1f7ca09b6c69264dc6421?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d70bea2070d1f7ca09b6c69264dc6421?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\"><a href='https://www.cadlonline.com' rel='external nofollow' class='url'>Justice For Chinese</a></b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/#comment-949140\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-12T01:00:35+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 12, 2017 at 1:00 am\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>Arch,</p>\n<p>Brilliant writing! I&#8217;ve been away from California for the last two years, but I lived there for the last 25 years prior to that and I noticed the state going downhill also.  It&#8217;s still a beautiful state in parts and I hope things can be turned around.  I would like to live there again someday. </p>\n<p>I expressed similar hopes in my article on Trump, saying I hoped he would awaken to the Jews and what they do, their motives and their frequently malicious and underhanded ways.  I am not going to say this will happen.  It probably won&#8217;t, but the thought of that happening reminds me of one of the most interesting things I ever read from the brilliant historian David Irving.</p>\n<p>In 1990 or 1991 David Irving became aware of the existence of the diaries of Germany&#8217;s Josef Goebbels (extending 25 years or longer).  Diaries are an excellent source of reliable material.  They are personal and people don&#8217;t usually lie in their own diaries.  Irving went to the Moscow archive and located the thousands of pages of Goebbels diaries (on a type of microfilm, actually glass plates) extending over decades.  They had laid there untouched since being placed there decades earlier, at the end of the war.  Being an expert on WW II and the questions that still remained unanswered, Irving knew what he was interested in and where to focus his search in the diaries.  He returned to London and began reporting in the Sunday Times, I believe, what he had found.  The &#8220;shit hit the fan&#8221; so to speak as the Jews began attacking Irving, because they knew he would write the truth and that would include anything that would reflect badly on them.  While others bow down to their pressure, David Irving never did.  The story continues a few years later with Jews pressuring the publisher of his award nominated book on Goebbels, to trash the book and not publish it.  The story hit the media and David Irving&#8217;s publisher caved in to the Jews, and then didn&#8217;t publish the book, even after they had nominated that same book for awards.  </p>\n<p>Here is a television debate on what happened.</p>\n<p>Christopher Hitchens on Charlie Rose &#8211; On David Irving&#8217;s controversial biography (May 8, 1996)<br/>\n<a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fdxTsWXZdFc\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=fdxTsWXZdFc</a></p>\n<p>I think this story is very interesting and that is why I repeated it here, but that is not the main point I wanted to make.  David Irving relays that there was a war going on between World Jewry and Germany, including propaganda, boycotts, assassinations and more, and Jews carried out all these things while Germany was curtailing the rights of German Jews and encouraging them to leave Germany by making life difficult for them.  The fact that Jews played a central and leading role, a hostile role against Germany, leading up to the war has been hidden from the media by Jews.  Like the fact that they were the leaders of the murderous USSR, their peacetime war on Germany has been hidden from the newspapers and most history books, leaving the impression with most people that completely innocent Jews were being targeted again.  David Irving&#8217;s biographies of Goebbels and Churchill put that claim to rest, as do Solzhenitsyn&#8217;s books on the USSR and Russian President Putin&#8217;s speech on the Jews leading role in the USSR.  Jews want to be seen as having no role in these nasty years, other than that of victim, and not be seen as a victimizer.  David Irving has exposed the Jews leading role in ratcheting up the hostilities between the worlds countries prior to 1939 and their leading role in pushing the world into WW II, and they don&#8217;t like it.</p>\n<p>Irving reveals that Josef Goebbels was more hostile, or aggressive towards Jews than Hitler.  Once you become aware of what they were doing, you might not blame him.  Irving shows that Hitler sometimes intervened on their behalf, and that enrages the Jews, who claimed for decades that Hitler &#8220;ordered the holocaust&#8221;.  David Irving put that lie to rest by offering a cash reward to any historian that could show him that order.  No such order has ever been found.</p>\n<p>But one of the most interesting things about Josef Goebbels are his attitudes prior to becoming a leader in the National Socialist Party.  Irving shows the Josef Goebbels grew up in a house next to Jewish neighbors and that Goebbels and his family were good friends with their Jewish neighbors.  Later David Irving goes into Goebbels love life and from Goebbels&#8217; diaries, gets to know that life intimately.  He learns of Goebbels Jewish girlfriend and Irving reveals how Goebbels criticizes another girlfriend when she says something mildly &#8220;anti-semitic&#8221;.   When I first read of this, I was astounded.  This is in stark contrast to how Josef Goebbels views Jews only a few years later.  And this is the thought that comes into my head.  Will Trump awaken and see the hostile Jews for what they are too?  Could it happen during his presidency, or will it happen after he&#8217;s out of office, or will it never happen?  Trump could crush his own negative thoughts of Jews if he ever began to feel that way, especially because they&#8217;re in his family now.  It&#8217;s fascinating to see how Goebbels attitudes change toward Jews as Irving unfolds the Jews relentless hostility towards Germany and its leadership. </p>\n<p>I have a soft spot for Josef Goebbels.  in the last few months of the war when the horror of that war reached its peak for Germans and all seemed lost, with millions fleeing the gang raping Soviets westward and British and American bombers murdering thousands every night, over 100,000 in two hours in Dresden, the German spirit never gave way.  My mother told me of how she thought Germany would win the war right up to almost the very end.  Goebbels would speak directly to the German women and tell them they were living in the most important time in all history and despite all the hardship and suffering, Germany would win the war. </p>\n<p>One of the saddest things I ever read is when Josef Goebbels received the news that the British and Americans had demolished Dresden, killing hundreds of thousands of refugees that had flooded into the city.  I read that on hearing the news, Goebbels eyes welled up with tears.  At the very moment I read that, my eyes welled up too.       </p>\n<p>Shortly after the lost Battle of Stalingrad and the British and American insistence on Germany&#8217;s &#8220;unconditional surrender&#8221;, Josef Goebbels gives Germany&#8217;s answer</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZRvafKSJ1ls\" rel=\"nofollow\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZRvafKSJ1ls</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-content -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"reply\"><a rel='nofollow' class='comment-reply-link' href='https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/?replytocom=948883#respond' onclick='return addComment.moveForm( \"div-comment-948883\", \"948883\", \"respond\", \"62328\" )' aria-label='Reply to Peter'>Reply</a></div>\t\t\t</article><!-- .comment-body -->\n<ol class=\"children\">\n\t\t<li id=\"comment-948888\" class=\"comment odd alt depth-2\">\n\t\t\t<article id=\"div-comment-948888\" class=\"comment-body\">\n\t\t\t\t<footer class=\"comment-meta\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-author vcard\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt='' src='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d1dc2c6de162b3835238ea646853ac24?s=60&#038;d=mm&#038;r=pg' srcset='https://secure.gravatar.com/avatar/d1dc2c6de162b3835238ea646853ac24?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x' class='avatar avatar-60 photo' height='60' width='60'/>\t\t\t\t\t\t<b class=\"fn\">TheRealOriginalJoe</b> <span class=\"says\">says:</span>\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-author -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-metadata\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.darkmoon.me/2017/a-cry-from-california-god-help-us-all/#comment-948888\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<time datetime=\"2017-03-09T09:51:58+00:00\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMarch 9, 2017 at 9:51 am\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</time>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t</a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div><!-- .comment-metadata -->\n\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</footer><!-- .comment-meta -->\n\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"comment-content\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<p>I feel your pain, Peter. Stephan Thorne, former female, the first transgender male San Francisco Police Department officer \u2014 once a pretty gal, now a guy with a mustache.\n\nIs it any wonder that people in California are a bit confused?\n\nI was getting my granddaughter to sleep and we were lying in bed together reading stories. She suddenly got this funny look on her face and said, \u201cLet\u2019s play a tickle game.\u201d She began naming my body parts. I said that I didn\u2019t like tickle games and I put the whole thing to a stop by reading her another story. But the incident disturbed me. She spends half the time with her father, although she is barely three years old. He without a doubt is a heavy watcher of porn and is well acquainted with the wild side of Los Angeles. He is obviously sexually turned on by her. Smitten with his own daughter.\n\nShould an adult male who watches porn be playing tickling game with his three year old daughter? That\u2019s a rhetorical question. I already know the answer. I\u2019m talking about my granddaughter here\u2026 and I can tell you, I don\u2019t like this situation one little bit.\n\nBut what can I do about it?\n\nEven if I could do something about this guy, my granddaughter is probably better off where she is than if she got taken into protective custody. She\u2019s a blonde, you see, and I guess that carries an extra price. YUCK!!\n\nWe\u2019ll know whether Trump is going to succeed or fail in cleaning the swamp when it comes to prosecution of certain high profile people in the Clinton camp like John Podesta, who is rumored to be an evil pedophile. I pray that the Washington pedophile ring aligned with the Clintons faces justice soon\u2026 very soon. This is urgent!!\n\n\u2014 \u00a7 \u2014\n\nMy Jewish mother in law lived in New York and would come to visit once a year with a suitcase of frozen food because she wouldn\u2019t eat in my house since I was too treif, that is non-kosher. This was although my mother-in-law was not religious and actually disliked Jews. Since Jews were the only people she knew, she basically disliked everyone. So\u2026 one year she is coming over to my place for Passover and I go to a deli and get very fancy Passover food to have a Seder. She arrives from her hotel with her normal look of disgust on her face, but once we sat down for the Seder meal she went into flip out mode.\n\n\u201cWhat is this,\u201d she screams, \u201chave you people turned into Lubovitchers?\u201d\n\nThat ended that.
